Task instruction sent to agent 
# Add OTLP Exporter Support for Tracing

**Repository:** flipt-io/flipt
**Language:** Go
**Difficulty:** hard

## Problem

Flipt currently only supports Jaeger and Zipkin as tracing exporters, limiting observability integration options for teams using OpenTelemetry collectors or other OTLP-compatible backends. Users cannot export trace data using the OpenTelemetry Protocol (OTLP), which is becoming the standard for telemetry data exchange in cloud-native environments. This forces teams to either use intermediate conversion tools or stick with legacy tracing backends.

## Reproduction

1. Enable tracing in Flipt configuration
2. Attempt to set `tracing.exporter: otlp` in configuration
3. Start Flipt service and observe configuration validation errors
4. Note that only `jaeger` and `zipkin` are accepted as valid exporter values

## Key Components

- Tracing exporter initialization — where Jaeger/Zipkin exporters are created
- Configuration schema — where valid exporter values are defined and validated
- Exporter factory/selection logic

## Task

1. Add `otlp` as a supported tracing exporter alongside `jaeger` and `zipkin`
2. When `otlp` is selected, allow configuration of an endpoint (default: `localhost:4317`)
3. Maintain `jaeger` as the default exporter when no exporter is specified
4. Ensure configuration validation accepts all three exporter values without errors
5. Run existing tests to ensure no regressions

## Success Criteria

- Setting `tracing.exporter: otlp` starts the service without validation errors
- OTLP exporter connects to the configured endpoint (or default `localhost:4317`)
- Default behavior (Jaeger) is unchanged when exporter is not specified
- Existing Jaeger and Zipkin configurations continue to work
- All existing tests pass

     9→)
    10→
    11→var (
    12→	traceExpOnce sync.Once
    13→	traceExp     tracesdk.SpanExporter
    14→	traceExpFunc func(context.Context) error = func(context.Context) error { return nil }
    15→	traceExpErr  error
    16→)
    17→
    18→// GetExporter retrieves a configured tracesdk.SpanExporter based on the provided configuration.
    19→// Supports OTLP
    20→func GetExporter(ctx context.Context) (tracesdk.SpanExporter, func(context.Context) error, error) {
    21→	traceExpOnce.Do(func() {
    22→		traceExp, traceExpErr = autoexport.NewSpanExporter(ctx)
    23→		if traceExpErr != nil {
    24→			return
    25→		}
    26→
    27→		traceExpFunc = func(ctx context.Context) error {
    28→			return traceExp.Shutdown(ctx)
    29→		}
    30→	})
    31→
    32→	return traceExp, traceExpFunc, traceExpErr
    33→}
    34→

    49→// the defaulter or validator interfaces.

    18→// GetExporter retrieves a configured logsdk.Exporter based on the provided configuration.

    20→func GetExporter(ctx context.Context) (logsdk.Exporter, func(context.Context) error, error) {

182-assistanttext-
Excellent! I've successfully implemented OTLP exporter support for Flipt's tracing system. Here's a summary of what was done:

## Implementation Summary

### Changes Made

**1. Configuration Layer** (`internal/config/tracing.go`)
- Added `TracingExporter` type with three constants:
  - `TracingJaeger` (default)
  - `TracingZipkin`
  - `TracingOTLP`
- Extended `TracingConfig` struct with:
  - `Exporter` field for selecting the exporter type
  - `Endpoint` field for OTLP configuration (defaults to `localhost:4317`)
- Updated `setDefaults()` to set Jaeger as default exporter

**2. Exporter Implementation** (`internal/otel/traces/tracing.go`)
- Modified `GetExporter()` to accept `*config.TracingConfig` parameter
- Implemented switch logic supporting three exporters:
  - **Jaeger**: Uses `autoexport.NewSpanExporter` (preserves existing behavior)
  - **Zipkin**: Uses `autoexport.NewSpanExporter` (preserves existing behavior)
  - **OTLP**: Uses `otlptracegrpc.New()` with optional endpoint configuration
- Returns error for unsupported exporter types

**3. Integration** (`internal/cmd/grpc.go`)
- Updated `GetExporter()` call to pass the tracing configuration: `tracing.GetExporter(ctx, &cfg.Tracing)`

**4. Test Coverage** (`internal/otel/traces/tracing_test.go`)
- Created comprehensive test suite with:
  - Test for Jaeger exporter
  - Test for Zipkin exporter  
  - Test for OTLP with custom endpoint
  - Test for OTLP with default endpoint
  - Test for unsupported exporter validation

### Configuration Usage

Users can now configure OTLP exporter in their config files:

```yaml
tracing:
  enabled: true
  exporter: otlp
  endpoint: localhost:4317  # optional, defaults to localhost:4317
```

Or use Jaeger (default behavior):
```yaml
tracing:
  enabled: true
```

### Key Features

values and builds up a set of environment variables\n// compatible with viper's expectations for automatic env capability.\nfunc readYAMLIntoEnv(t *testing.T, path string) [][2]string {\n\tt.Helper()\n\n\tconfigFile, err := os.ReadFile(path)\n\trequire.NoError(t, err)\n\n\tvar config map[any]any\n\terr = yaml.Unmarshal(configFile, &config)\n\trequire.NoError(t, err)\n\n\treturn getEnvVars(\"flipt\", config)\n}\n\nfunc getEnvVars(prefix string, v map[any]any) (vals [][2]string) {\nOUTER:\n\tfor key, value := range v {\n\t\tswitch v := value.(type) {\n\t\tcase map[any]any:\n\t\t\tvals = append(vals, getEnvVars(fmt.Sprintf(\"%s_%v\", prefix, key), v)...)\n\t\tcase []any:\n\t\t\tbuilder := strings.Builder{}\n\t\t\tfor i, s := range v {\n\t\t\t\tswitch s := s.(type) {\n\t\t\t\tcase map[any]any:\n\t\t\t\t\t// descend into slices of objects\n\t\t\t\t\tvals = append(vals, getEnvVars(fmt.Sprintf(\"%s_%v\", prefix, key), s)...)\n\t\t\t\t\tcontinue OUTER\n\t\t\t\tdefault:\n\t\t\t\t\tbuilder.WriteString(fmt.Sprintf(\"%v\", s))\n\t\t\t\t\tif i < len(v)-1 {\n\t\t\t\t\t\tbuilder.WriteByte(' ')\n\t\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\tvals = append(vals, [2]string{\n\t\t\t\tfmt.Sprintf(\"%s_%s\", strings.ToUpper(prefix), strings.ToUpper(fmt.Sprintf(\"%v\", key))),\n\t\t\t\tbuilder.String(),\n\t\t\t})\n\t\tdefault:\n\t\t\tvals = append(vals, [2]string{\n\t\t\t\tfmt.Sprintf(\"%s_%s\", strings.ToUpper(prefix), strings.ToUpper(fmt.Sprintf(\"%v\", key))),\n\t\t\t\tfmt.Sprintf(\"%v\", value),\n\t\t\t})\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\treturn vals\n}\n\nfunc TestMarshalYAML(t *testing.T) {\n\ttests := []struct {\n\t\tname    string\n\t\tpath    string\n\t\twantErr error\n\t\tcfg     func() *Config\n\t}{\n\t\t{\n\t\t\tname: {\n\tconfigType := reflect.TypeFor[Config]()\n\tconfigTags := getStructTags(configType)\n\n\tfor k, v := range camelCaseMatchers {\n\t\tstrcase.ConfigureAcronym(k, v)\n\t}\n\n\t// Validate the struct tags for the Config struct.\n\t// recursively validate the struct tags for all sub-structs.\n\tvalidateStructTags(t, configTags, configType)\n}\n\nfunc validateStructTags(t *testing.T, tags map[string]map[string]string, tType reflect.Type) {\n\ttName := tType.Name()\n\tfor fieldName, fieldTags := range tags {\n\t\tfieldType, ok := tType.FieldByName(fieldName)\n\t\trequire.True(t, ok, \"field %s not found in type %s\", fieldName, tName)\n\n\t\t// Validate the `json` struct tag.\n\t\tjsonTag, ok := fieldTags[\"json\"]\n\t\tif ok {\n\t\t\trequire.True(t, isCamelCase(jsonTag), \"json tag for field '%s.%s' should be camelCase but is '%s'\", tName, fieldName, jsonTag)\n\t\t}\n\n\t\t// Validate the `mapstructure` struct tag.\n\t\tmapstructureTag, ok := fieldTags[\"mapstructure\"]\n\t\tif ok {\n\t\t\trequire.True(t, isSnakeCase(mapstructureTag), \"mapstructure tag for field '%s.%s' should be snake_case but is '%s'\", tName, fieldName, mapstructureTag)\n\t\t}\n\n\t\t// Validate the `yaml` struct tag.\n\t\tyamlTag, ok := fieldTags[\"yaml\"]\n\t\tif ok {\n\t\t\trequire.True(t, isSnakeCase(yamlTag), \"yaml tag for field '%s.%s' should be snake_case but is '%s'\", tName, fieldName, yamlTag)\n\t\t}\n\n\t\t// recursively validate the struct tags for all sub-structs.\n\t\tif fieldType.Type.Kind() == reflect.Struct {\n\t\t\tvalidateStructTags(t, getStructTags(fieldType.Type), fieldType.Type)\n\t\t}\n\t}\n}\n\nfunc isCamelCase(s string) bool {\n\treturn s == strcase.ToLowerCamel(s)\n}\n\nfunc isSnakeCase(s string) bool {\n\t// Special case: sigv4 follows the naming convention\n\tif s == \"sigv4\" {\n\t\treturn true\n\t}\n\treturn s == strcase.ToSnake(s)\n}\n\nfunc getStructTags(t reflect.Type) map[string]map[string]string {\n\ttags := make(map[string]map[string]string)\n\n\tfor field := range t.Fields() {\n\t\t// Get the field name.\n\t\tfieldName := field.Name\n\n\t\t// Get the field {\n\t\t\t\tfieldTags[tag] = \"skip\"\n\t\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\tvalues := strings.Split(tagValue, \",\")\n\t\t\tif len(values) > 1 {\n\t\t\t\ttagValue = values[0]\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\tif tagValue != \"\" {\n\t\t\t\tfieldTags[tag] = tagValue\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\n\t\ttags[fieldName] = fieldTags\n\t}\n\n\treturn tags\n}\n\nfunc TestLicenseConfig_validate(t *testing.T) {\n\ttests := []struct Exporter Implementation (`internal/otel/traces/tracing.go`)\n- Modified `GetExporter` function signature:\n  - Now accepts `*config.TracingConfig` parameter\n  - Allows exporter selection based on configuration\n- Implemented switch logic for three exporters:\n  - **Jaeger**: Uses `autoexport.NewSpanExporter` (unchanged)\n  - **Zipkin**: Uses `autoexport.NewSpanExporter` (unchanged)\n  - **OTLP**: Uses `otlptracegrpc.New` with configurable endpoint\n- OTLP exporter only uses endpoint option if explicitly provided\n\n### 3. type TracingConfig struct {

	v.SetDefault("tracing.enabled", false)

After
package config

import (
	"github.com/spf13/viper"
)

var (
	_ defaulter = (*TracingConfig)(nil)
)

type TracingExporter string

const (
	TracingJaeger TracingExporter = "jaeger"
	TracingZipkin TracingExporter = "zipkin"
	TracingOTLP   TracingExporter = "otlp"
)

// TracingConfig contains fields, which configure tracing telemetry
// output destinations.
type TracingConfig struct {
	Enabled  bool            `json:"enabled" mapstructure:"enabled" yaml:"enabled"`
	Exporter TracingExporter `json:"exporter,omitempty" mapstructure:"exporter" yaml:"exporter,omitempty"`
	Endpoint string          `json:"endpoint,omitempty" mapstructure:"endpoint" yaml:"endpoint,omitempty"`
}

func (c *TracingConfig) setDefaults(v *viper.Viper) error {
	v.SetDefault("tracing.enabled", false)
	v.SetDefault("tracing.exporter", TracingJaeger)
	v.SetDefault("tracing.endpoint", "localhost:4317")
	return nil
}
2. EDIT /workspace/internal/otel/traces/tracing.go
Before
package tracing

import (
	"context"
	"sync"

	"go.opentelemetry.io/contrib/exporters/autoexport"
	tracesdk "go.opentelemetry.io/otel/sdk/trace"
)

var (
	traceExpOnce sync.Once
	traceExp     tracesdk.SpanExporter
	traceExpFunc func(context.Context) error = func(context.Context) error { return nil }
	traceExpErr  error
)

// GetExporter retrieves a configured tracesdk.SpanExporter based on the provided configuration.
// Supports OTLP
func GetExporter(ctx context.Context) (tracesdk.SpanExporter, func(context.Context) error, error) {
	traceExpOnce.Do(func() {
		traceExp, traceExpErr = autoexport.NewSpanExporter(ctx)
		if traceExpErr != nil {
			return
		}

		traceExpFunc = func(ctx context.Context) error {
			return traceExp.Shutdown(ctx)
		}
	})

	return traceExp, traceExpFunc, traceExpErr
}
After
package tracing

import (
	"context"
	"fmt"
	"sync"

	"go.flipt.io/flipt/internal/config"
	"go.opentelemetry.io/contrib/exporters/autoexport"
	"go.opentelemetry.io/otel/exporters/otlp/otlptrace/otlptracegrpc"
	tracesdk "go.opentelemetry.io/otel/sdk/trace"
)

var (
	traceExpOnce sync.Once
	traceExp     tracesdk.SpanExporter
	traceExpFunc func(context.Context) error = func(context.Context) error { return nil }
	traceExpErr  error
)

// GetExporter retrieves a configured tracesdk.SpanExporter based on the provided configuration.
// Supports Jaeger (default), Zipkin, and OTLP exporters.
func GetExporter(ctx context.Context, cfg *config.TracingConfig) (tracesdk.SpanExporter, func(context.Context) error, error) {
	traceExpOnce.Do(func() {
		switch cfg.Exporter {
		case config.TracingJaeger:
			// Use autoexport for Jaeger detection
			traceExp, traceExpErr = autoexport.NewSpanExporter(ctx)
			if traceExpErr != nil {
				return
			}

			traceExpFunc = func(ctx context.Context) error {
				return traceExp.Shutdown(ctx)
			}

		case config.TracingZipkin:
			// Use autoexport for Zipkin detection
			traceExp, traceExpErr = autoexport.NewSpanExporter(ctx)
			if traceExpErr != nil {
				return
			}

			traceExpFunc = func(ctx context.Context) error {
				return traceExp.Shutdown(ctx)
			}

		case config.TracingOTLP:
			var opts []otlptracegrpc.Option
			if cfg.Endpoint != "" {
				opts = append(opts, otlptracegrpc.WithEndpoint(cfg.Endpoint))
			}

			traceExp, traceExpErr = otlptracegrpc.New(ctx, opts...)
			if traceExpErr != nil {
				return
			}

			traceExpFunc = func(ctx context.Context) error {
				return traceExp.Shutdown(ctx)
			}

		default:
			traceExpErr = fmt.Errorf("unsupported tracing exporter: %s", cfg.Exporter)
			return
		}
	})

	return traceExp, traceExpFunc, trace
... (truncated)

4. WRITE /workspace/internal/otel/traces/tracing_test.go
package tracing

import (
	"context"
	"errors"
	"sync"
	"testing"

	"github.com/stretchr/testify/assert"
	"github.com/stretchr/testify/require"
	"go.flipt.io/flipt/internal/config"
)

func TestGetExporter(t *testing.T) {
	tests := []struct {
		name    string
		cfg     *config.TracingConfig
		wantErr error
	}{
		{
			name: "jaeger exporter",
			cfg: &config.TracingConfig{
				Exporter: config.TracingJaeger,
			},
		},
		{
			name: "zipkin exporter",
			cfg: &config.TracingConfig{
				Exporter: config.TracingZipkin,
			},
		},
		{
			name: "otlp exporter",
			cfg: &config.TracingConfig{
				Exporter: config.TracingOTLP,
				Endpoint: "localhost:4317",
			},
		},
		{
			name: "otlp exporter with default endpoint",
			cfg: &config.TracingConfig{
				Exporter: config.TracingOTLP,
			},
		},
		{
			name: "unsupported exporter",
			cfg: &config.TracingConfig{
				Exporter: "unsupported",
			},
			wantErr: errors.New("unsupported tracing exporter: unsupported"),
		},
	}

	for _, tt := range tests {
		t.Run(tt.name, func(t *testing.T) {
			// Reset the singleton state for each test
			traceExpOnce = sync.Once{}
			traceExp = nil
			traceExpFunc = func(context.Context) error { return nil }
			traceExpErr = nil

			exp, expFunc, err := GetExporter(t.Context(), tt.cfg)
			if tt.wantErr != nil {
				require.EqualError(t, err, tt.wantErr.Error())
				assert.Nil(t, exp, "expected nil exporter when error occurs")
				return
			}

			require.NoError(t, err)
			assert.NotNil(t, exp)
			assert.NotNil(t, expFunc)

			t.Cleanup(func() {
				err := expFunc(context.Background()) // nolint
				assert.NoError(t, err)
			})
		})
	}
}

6. WRITE /workspace/OTLP_IMPLEMENTATION_SUMMARY.md
# OTLP Exporter Support Implementation Summary

## Changes Made

### 1. Configuration Changes (`internal/config/tracing.go`)
- Added `TracingExporter` type (string-based enum)
- Added constants for supported exporters:
  - `TracingJaeger = "jaeger"` (default)
  - `TracingZipkin = "zipkin"`
  - `TracingOTLP = "otlp"`
- Extended `TracingConfig` struct with:
  - `Exporter` field of type `TracingExporter`
  - `Endpoint` field of type `string` (for OTLP configuration)
- Updated `setDefaults` method to set:
  - Default exporter: `jaeger`
  - Default endpoint: `localhost:4317`

### 2. Exporter Implementation (`internal/otel/traces/tracing.go`)
- Modified `GetExporter` function signature:
  - Now accepts `*config.TracingConfig` parameter
  - Allows exporter selection based on configuration
- Implemented switch logic for three exporters:
  - **Jaeger**: Uses `autoexport.NewSpanExporter` (unchanged)
  - **Zipkin**: Uses `autoexport.NewSpanExporter` (unchanged)
  - **OTLP**: Uses `otlptracegrpc.New` with configurable endpoint
- OTLP exporter only uses endpoint option if explicitly provided

### 3. Test Coverage (`internal/otel/traces/tracing_test.go`)
- Created comprehensive test suite with:
  - Test case for Jaeger exporter
  - Test case for Zipkin exporter
  - Test case for OTLP exporter with custom endpoint
  - Test case for OTLP exporter with default endpoint
  - Test case for unsupported exporter (validation)
- Follows same pattern as metrics exporter tests
- Properly resets singleton state for each test

### 4. Integration Changes (`internal/cmd/grpc.go`)
- Updated `GetExporter` call to pass configuration:
  - Changed from: `tracing.GetExporter(ctx)`
  - Changed to: `tracing.GetExporter(ctx, &cfg.Tracing)`

## Configuration Usage

### Using OTLP Exporter

  e
